## 4. EXPLICIT SSOT LOSS PROTOCOL
Р•СЃР»Рё РёСЃС‚РѕС‡РЅРёРє РёСЃС‚РёРЅС‹ РїРѕС‚РµСЂСЏРЅ, С‡Р°С‚ РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ РѕС‚РІРµС‚РёС‚СЊ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РїРѕ СЌС‚РѕРјСѓ РїСЂРѕС‚РѕРєРѕР»Сѓ:

## 6. NON-BYPASS MECHANISM
Р’РІРѕРґРёС‚СЃСЏ Р¶С‘СЃС‚РєР°СЏ Р»РѕРіРёРєР°, РєРѕС‚РѕСЂСѓСЋ С‡Р°С‚ РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ РїСЂРёРјРµРЅСЏС‚СЊ РєР°Рє СЂСѓР±РёР»СЊРЅРёРє.

### SSOT LOCK SWITCH

ROLE LOCK
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following role separation remains canonical and MUST NOT be lost:

- Master Agent = governance / final authority / policy / generation
- Orchestrator = routing / retry / deadline / coordination
- Execution Agents = task execution only
- Operator = hands only
- Human Approval = high-risk fallback only

If this role model is missing from the transmitted prompt,
handoff is incomplete.

11. QUARANTINE Р KILL-SWITCH
====================================================================================================================

ABSOLUTE RULE: quarantine РёРјРµРµС‚ РїСЂРёРѕСЂРёС‚РµС‚ РІС‹С€Рµ Р»СЋР±РѕРіРѕ execution flow.

| РўР РР“Р“Р•Р  | Р”Р•Р™РЎРўР’РР• | РџР РРћР РРўР•Рў |
|---------|---------|---------|

| Write РІРЅРµ scope | РќРµРјРµРґР»РµРЅРЅС‹Р№ quarantine | РљР РРўРР§Р•РЎРљРР™ |
| Repeat failure РІС‹С€Рµ РїРѕСЂРѕРіР° | quarantine + review | HIGH |

- РѕР±С…РѕРґРёС‚СЊ Р°СѓРґРёС‚РѕСЂР°;

13. UNSANCTIONED ACTION RULE

Р•СЃР»Рё РёСЃРїРѕР»РЅРёС‚РµР»СЊ РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРёР» Р·РЅР°С‡РёРјРѕРµ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІРёРµ Р±РµР· РїСЂРµРґРІР°СЂРёС‚РµР»СЊРЅРѕРіРѕ СЃРѕРіР»Р°СЃРѕРІР°РЅРёСЏ СЃ Р°СѓРґРёС‚РѕСЂРѕРј,
СЌС‚Рѕ Р°РІС‚РѕРјР°С‚РёС‡РµСЃРєРё СЃС‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ РЅР°СЂСѓС€РµРЅРёРµРј СѓРїСЂР°РІР»СЏСЋС‰РµРіРѕ РєРѕРЅС‚СѓСЂР°.

РђСѓРґРёС‚РѕСЂ РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ:

1. ROLE MODEL
====================================================================================================================

| DISPLAY ROLE | CANONICAL ENUM | RESPONSIBILITY | FORBIDDEN |
|-------------|----------------|----------------|-----------|
| РђРЅР°Р»РёС‚РёРє | ANALYST | С„РѕСЂРјРёСЂСѓРµС‚ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ; РіРѕС‚РѕРІРёС‚ revision; РіРѕС‚РѕРІРёС‚ corrective proposal; РЅРµ РёСЃРїРѕР»РЅСЏРµС‚ cloud actions | РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ governance-СЂРµС€РµРЅРёРµ; РёСЃРїРѕР»РЅСЏС‚СЊ cloud execution РєР°Рє С€С‚Р°С‚РЅС‹Р№ runtime |
| РђСѓРґРёС‚РѕСЂ | AUDITOR | РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°РµС‚ РёР»Рё Р±Р»РѕРєРёСЂСѓРµС‚ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ; РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°РµС‚ РёР»Рё РЅРµ РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°РµС‚ СЂРµР·СѓР»СЊС‚Р°С‚; РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡Р°РµС‚ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РёР№ РґРѕРїСѓСЃС‚РёРјС‹Р№ С…РѕРґ | РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅСЏС‚СЊ СЂРѕР»СЊ РјР°СЂС€СЂСѓС‚РёР·Р°С‚РѕСЂР°; РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅСЏС‚СЊ СЂРѕР»СЊ server-side writer; РѕР±С…РѕРґРёС‚СЊ evidence |
| Cloud Code | CLOUD_CODE | РёСЃРїРѕР»РЅСЏРµС‚ СѓР¶Рµ РѕРґРѕР±СЂРµРЅРЅСѓСЋ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ РїРѕ РєРѕРЅРєСЂРµС‚РЅРѕРјСѓ payload | РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ governance-СЂРµС€РµРЅРёРµ; С‡РёС‚Р°С‚СЊ ledger РєР°Рє РёСЃС‚РѕС‡РЅРёРє СЃС‚СЂР°С‚РµРіРёРё; РёСЃРїРѕР»РЅСЏС‚СЊ РЅРµСЂР°Р·СЂРµС€С‘РЅРЅС‹Р№ scope |
| Ledger Writer | LEDGER_WRITER | СЃРµСЂРІРµСЂРЅРѕ РїРёС€РµС‚ СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёСЏ РІ repo ledger РїРѕ canonical schema | РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ governance-СЂРµС€РµРЅРёСЏ; РјР°СЂС€СЂСѓС‚РёР·РёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РёР№ С…РѕРґ; РјРµРЅСЏС‚СЊ СЃС‚Р°СЂС‹Рµ СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёСЏ |
| Ledger Router | LEDGER_ROUTER | С‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚ РЅРѕРІРѕРµ ledger-СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёРµ; РѕРїСЂРµРґРµР»СЏРµС‚ Р°РґСЂРµСЃР°С‚Р° РїРѕ already-written audit decision; Р·Р°РїСѓСЃРєР°РµС‚ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РёР№ РєРѕРЅС‚СѓСЂ | РїРёСЃР°С‚СЊ governance-СЂРµС€РµРЅРёСЏ; РјРµРЅСЏС‚СЊ ledger history; РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ next actor РїРѕ СЃРѕР±СЃС‚РІРµРЅРЅРѕР№ Р»РѕРіРёРєРµ |
| РћРїРµСЂР°С‚РѕСЂ | OPERATOR | override; high-risk approval; final authority | normal routing; normal execution; normal post-audit acceptance |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
- ANALYST != CLOUD_CODE
- LEDGER_WRITER != LEDGER_ROUTER
- LEDGER_ROUTER != governance authority
- next handoff authority = ONLY AUDITOR
- operator override remains supreme

2. CANONICAL ENUM RULE
====================================================================================================================

Р’Рѕ РІСЃРµС… machine-readable РїРѕР»СЏС… РґРѕРїСѓСЃРєР°СЋС‚СЃСЏ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РёРµ canonical enum values РґР»СЏ СЂРѕР»РµР№:

- ANALYST
- AUDITOR
- CLOUD_CODE
- OPERATOR
- LEDGER_WRITER
- LEDGER_ROUTER
- NONE

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Human-readable display names РґРѕРїСѓСЃС‚РёРјС‹ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РІ narrative/documentation layer.
Machine-readable fields MUST use canonical enum values only.

====================================================================================================================
3. CANONICAL REPOSITORY OBJECTS
====================================================================================================================

| OBJECT | PURPOSE | MUTABILITY |
|--------|---------|------------|
| governance/exchange_ledger.csv | immutable event log | APPEND-ONLY |
| governance/dispatch_registry.json | routing/delivery state | MUTABLE |
| governance/transition_map.json | allowed transitions contract | VERSIONED |
| governance/ledger_schema.json | canonical ledger schema | VERSIONED |
| governance/router_payloads/ | optional materialized extracted payloads | MUTABLE / VERSIONED BY PROCESS |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Exchange-ledger is immutable event log.
Routing state MUST NOT be stored by rewriting prior ledger events.

====================================================================================================================
4. LEDGER IMMUTABILITY RULE
====================================================================================================================

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Exchange-ledger is APPEND-ONLY.

FORBIDDEN:
- update existing event rows
- delete event rows
- overwrite historical auditor decisions
- mutate previous task history
- rewrite prior next_actor_role
- use ledger as mutable state store
- store router retry counters inside historical ledger rows

If mutable delivery state is needed,
it MUST be stored in dispatch-registry, not in exchange-ledger.

====================================================================================================================
5. CANONICAL WRITE PATH
====================================================================================================================

Canonical autonomous ledger write path is:

SERVER-SIDE LEDGER WRITER
в†’ repo write
в†’ commit
в†’ repo factual confirmation

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Chat UI write is NOT canonical autonomous write path.

ALLOWED ONLY AS:
- operator emergency bootstrap
- explicit operator override
- temporary recovery action before server-side writer is operational

TARGET RULE:
Normal production ledger writes MUST be executed by server-side ledger writer.

====================================================================================================================
6. CANONICAL ROUTING PATH
====================================================================================================================

Canonical routing path is:

AUDITOR WRITES GOVERNANCE DECISION
в†’ LEDGER WRITER appends event
в†’ ledger commit occurs
в†’ LEDGER ROUTER reads appended event
в†’ LEDGER ROUTER validates allowed transition
в†’ LEDGER_ROUTER dispatches next actor
в†’ DISPATCH REGISTRY records delivery state

ABSOLUTE RULE:
LEDGER_ROUTER does not invent next actor.
LEDGER_ROUTER only executes already-written governance decision.

====================================================================================================================
7. MINIMUM REQUIRED LEDGER COLUMNS
====================================================================================================================

РљР°Р¶РґР°СЏ Р·Р°РїРёСЃСЊ exchange-ledger РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅР° СЃРѕРґРµСЂР¶Р°С‚СЊ РјРёРЅРёРјСѓРј:

| COLUMN | REQUIRED | DESCRIPTION |
|--------|----------|-------------|
| schema_version | YES | РІРµСЂСЃРёСЏ СЃС…РµРјС‹ ledger |
| event_id | YES | СѓРЅРёРєР°Р»СЊРЅС‹Р№ РёРґРµРЅС‚РёС„РёРєР°С‚РѕСЂ СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёСЏ |

| task_id | YES | СЃС‚Р°Р±РёР»СЊРЅС‹Р№ РёРґРµРЅС‚РёС„РёРєР°С‚РѕСЂ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Рё |

| step_name | YES | С€Р°Рі roadmap / task name |

| description | YES | РїРѕР»РЅРѕРµ СЃРѕРґРµСЂР¶Р°РЅРёРµ СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёСЏ |
| status | YES | СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РїРѕСЃР»Рµ СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёСЏ |

| next_expected_event | YES | РєР°РєРѕРµ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РµРµ СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёРµ РґРѕРїСѓСЃС‚РёРјРѕ |
| routing_decision_basis | YES | РѕСЃРЅРѕРІР°РЅРёРµ РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРёСЏ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РµРіРѕ С…РѕРґР° |
| commit_sha | YES | commit SHA СЂРµРїРѕР·РёС‚РѕСЂРёСЏ, РІ РєРѕС‚РѕСЂРѕРј СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёРµ Р·Р°С„РёРєСЃРёСЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Р—Р°РїРёСЃСЊ Р±РµР· С…РѕС‚СЏ Р±С‹ РѕРґРЅРѕРіРѕ required field = INVALID EVENT.

====================================================================================================================
8. RECOMMENDED LEDGER COLUMNS
====================================================================================================================

| COLUMN | STATUS | DESCRIPTION |
|--------|--------|-------------|
| task_phase | RECOMMENDED | PRE_ACTION / EXECUTION / POST_ACTION / CLOSURE |
| artifact_ref | RECOMMENDED | СЃСЃС‹Р»РєР° РЅР° Р°СЂС‚РµС„Р°РєС‚ |
| proof_ref | RECOMMENDED | СЃСЃС‹Р»РєР° РЅР° proof |
| writer_actor | RECOMMENDED | РєС‚Рѕ С„РёР·РёС‡РµСЃРєРё РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРёР» Р·Р°РїРёСЃСЊ |
| dispatch_id | RECOMMENDED | СЃРІСЏР·РєР° СЃ dispatch-registry |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Recommended fields strengthen traceability but do not replace required fields.

====================================================================================================================
9. EVENT ID RULE
====================================================================================================================

| RULE | REQUIREMENT |
|------|-------------|
| uniqueness | event_id unique globally |
| stability | event_id never reused |
| format | machine-readable stable identifier |
| parent linkage | every non-root event must point to parent_event_id |

EXAMPLE:
- EVT-000001
- EVT-000002

ROOT RULE:
First event in a chain may use:
- ROOT
or
- NONE
as parent_event_id only if explicitly allowed by schema.

====================================================================================================================
10. NEXT ACTOR AUTHORITY RULE
====================================================================================================================

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Field next_actor_role is assigned ONLY by AUDITOR or OPERATOR override.

FORBIDDEN:
- ANALYST assigning final next_actor_role by own authority
- LEDGER_ROUTER inferring governance next actor from heuristics
- CLOUD_CODE deciding who moves next
- LEDGER_WRITER changing next_actor_role during write

ALLOWED next_actor_role values:

- ANALYST
- AUDITOR
- CLOUD_CODE
- OPERATOR
- NONE

Meaning:
- ANALYST = revision / next proposal / corrective work
- AUDITOR = pre/post review required
- CLOUD_CODE = execution allowed
- OPERATOR = explicit human intervention required
- NONE = chain terminal state

====================================================================================================================
11. NEXT EXPECTED EVENT RULE
====================================================================================================================

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Every event MUST declare next_expected_event.

This field defines the single canonical expected next stage.

Allowed values come only from canonical event type model.

FORBIDDEN:
- blank next_expected_event
- free-text invented event names
- multiple conflicting next_expected_event values in one event
- router replacing next_expected_event with its own guess

====================================================================================================================
12. ROUTING DECISION BASIS RULE
====================================================================================================================

Field routing_decision_basis is mandatory.

Allowed basis values:

| VALUE | MEANING |
|-------|---------|
| AUDITOR_DECISION | next step assigned by auditor |
| AUDITOR_CONDITIONAL_APPROVAL | next step assigned by auditor with conditions |
| AUDITOR_REWORK_DECISION | next step assigned by auditor for revision/rework |
| OPERATOR_OVERRIDE | next step assigned by operator |
| TERMINAL_STATE | no next actor required |
| SCHEMA_ENFORCEMENT | router validated already-assigned path against schema |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
LEDGER_ROUTER may use SCHEMA_ENFORCEMENT only for validation, not for governance invention.

====================================================================================================================
13. COMMIT SHA RULE
====================================================================================================================

Each ledger event MUST be bound to repository fact through commit_sha.

ABSOLUTE RULE:
No ledger event is canonical until:
- event is written to repo
- commit exists
- commit_sha is known

FORBIDDEN:
- in-memory-only event
- chat-only event
- event without repo confirmation
- event without commit_sha

====================================================================================================================
14. EVENT TYPE MODEL
====================================================================================================================

Allowed canonical event_type:

| EVENT TYPE | ROLE NORMALLY WRITES IT |
|------------|-------------------------|
| TASK_PROPOSED | ANALYST |
| TASK_REVISED | ANALYST |
| TASK_APPROVED | AUDITOR |
| TASK_APPROVED_WITH_CONDITIONS | AUDITOR |
| TASK_REVISION_REQUIRED | AUDITOR |
| TASK_REJECTED | AUDITOR |
| EXECUTION_STARTED | CLOUD_CODE or LEDGER_WRITER on behalf of execution contour |
| EXECUTION_FINISHED | CLOUD_CODE or LEDGER_WRITER on behalf of execution contour |
| RESULT_ACCEPTED | AUDITOR |
| RESULT_ACCEPTED_WITH_REMARKS | AUDITOR |
| RESULT_REWORK_REQUIRED | AUDITOR |
| RESULT_REJECTED | AUDITOR |
| TASK_CLOSED | AUDITOR |
| OPERATOR_OVERRIDE | OPERATOR |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Free-form event types are forbidden unless SSOT is updated first.

====================================================================================================================
15. STATUS MODEL
====================================================================================================================

Allowed canonical status:

| STATUS | MEANING |
|--------|---------|
| OPEN | chain active |
| IN_REVIEW | waiting for auditor review |
| APPROVED_FOR_EXECUTION | execution allowed |
| APPROVED_WITH_CONDITIONS | execution allowed under conditions |
| REVISION_REQUIRED | revision required |
| REJECTED | rejected |
| EXECUTED_PENDING_AUDIT | execution finished, waiting post-audit |
| ACCEPTED | accepted |
| ACCEPTED_WITH_REMARKS | accepted with remarks |
| CLOSED | task closed |
| OVERRIDE | operator override |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Status must match event_type semantics.

====================================================================================================================
16. ALLOWED TRANSITION MAP
====================================================================================================================

ABSOLUTE RULE:
LEDGER_ROUTER MUST validate every event against allowed transition map before dispatch.

Canonical transition map:

| CURRENT EVENT TYPE | NEXT ACTOR ROLE | NEXT EXPECTED EVENT |
|--------------------|-----------------|---------------------|
| TASK_PROPOSED | AUDITOR | TASK_APPROVED or TASK_APPROVED_WITH_CONDITIONS or TASK_REVISION_REQUIRED or TASK_REJECTED |
| TASK_REVISED | AUDITOR | TASK_APPROVED or TASK_APPROVED_WITH_CONDITIONS or TASK_REVISION_REQUIRED or TASK_REJECTED |
| TASK_APPROVED | CLOUD_CODE | EXECUTION_STARTED |
| TASK_APPROVED_WITH_CONDITIONS | CLOUD_CODE | EXECUTION_STARTED |
| TASK_REVISION_REQUIRED | ANALYST | TASK_REVISED |
| TASK_REJECTED | ANALYST or NONE | TASK_REVISED or NONE |
| EXECUTION_STARTED | CLOUD_CODE | EXECUTION_FINISHED |
| EXECUTION_FINISHED | AUDITOR | RESULT_ACCEPTED or RESULT_ACCEPTED_WITH_REMARKS or RESULT_REWORK_REQUIRED or RESULT_REJECTED |
| RESULT_ACCEPTED | AUDITOR | TASK_CLOSED |
| RESULT_ACCEPTED_WITH_REMARKS | AUDITOR | TASK_CLOSED |
| RESULT_REWORK_REQUIRED | ANALYST | TASK_REVISED |
| RESULT_REJECTED | ANALYST or OPERATOR | TASK_REVISED or OPERATOR_OVERRIDE |
| TASK_CLOSED | ANALYST or NONE | TASK_PROPOSED or NONE |
| OPERATOR_OVERRIDE | OPERATOR or ANALYST or AUDITOR or CLOUD_CODE | explicitly specified by override |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
If event transition is not in transition map:
- routing forbidden
- execution forbidden
- dispatch_status = BLOCKED in dispatch registry
- escalation required

====================================================================================================================
17. ANALYST CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

ANALYST РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ:
- С‡РёС‚Р°С‚СЊ РјР°СЂС€СЂСѓС‚ РёР· MASTER PROMPT;
- С‡РёС‚Р°С‚СЊ С„Р°РєС‚ РёР· repository/state/artifacts;
- С„РѕСЂРјРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ TASK_PROPOSED or TASK_REVISED;
- РЅРµ РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ execution СЃР°РјРѕСЃС‚РѕСЏС‚РµР»СЊРЅРѕ;
- РЅРµ РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ final acceptance;
- РЅРµ Р·Р°РєСЂС‹РІР°С‚СЊ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ;
- РЅРµ РїРёСЃР°С‚СЊ governance fiction.

ANALYST is not С€С‚Р°С‚РЅС‹Р№ РёСЃРїРѕР»РЅРёС‚РµР»СЊ cloud actions.
CLOUD_CODE is the execution runtime.

====================================================================================================================
18. AUDITOR CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

AUDITOR РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ:
- РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ РёР»Рё Р±Р»РѕРєРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ;
- РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ next_actor_role;
- РЅР°Р·РЅР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ next_expected_event;
- С„РѕСЂРјСѓР»РёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ routing_decision_basis;
- РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ РёР»Рё РЅРµ РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ СЂРµР·СѓР»СЊС‚Р°С‚;
- Р·Р°РєСЂС‹РІР°С‚СЊ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ РїСЂРё РїРѕР»РѕР¶РёС‚РµР»СЊРЅРѕРј Р·Р°РІРµСЂС€РµРЅРёРё.

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Without auditor-written handoff, LEDGER_ROUTER MUST NOT dispatch autonomous next step.

====================================================================================================================
19. CLOUD CODE CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

CLOUD_CODE MUST receive:
- concrete task_id
- concrete expected event
- extracted payload
- allowed scope
- relevant artifact refs
- relevant proof refs if required

CLOUD_CODE MUST NOT receive raw full CSV as primary task contract.

FORBIDDEN:
- using entire ledger as primary execution prompt
- deducing roadmap from raw ledger history
- selecting arbitrary task from CSV without routed payload
- expanding scope beyond auditor-approved event chain

====================================================================================================================
20. LEDGER ROUTER CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

LEDGER_ROUTER РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ:
- С‡РёС‚Р°С‚СЊ newly committed ledger event;
- РІР°Р»РёРґРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ schema_version;
- РІР°Р»РёРґРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ required fields;
- РІР°Р»РёРґРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ transition against transition map;
- РѕРїСЂРµРґРµР»РёС‚СЊ dispatch target from next_actor_role;
- РёР·РІР»РµС‡СЊ task-specific payload;
- РїРµСЂРµРґР°С‚СЊ payload only to assigned next actor;
- Р·Р°РїРёСЃР°С‚СЊ delivery state in dispatch-registry.

LEDGER_ROUTER MUST NOT:
- edit exchange-ledger history;
- assign next actor by itself;
- merge writer and router state;
- bypass auditor decision;
- dispatch if transition invalid;
- dispatch if required fields missing;
- dispatch if commit confirmation absent.

====================================================================================================================
21. LEDGER WRITER CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

LEDGER_WRITER РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ:
- РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°С‚СЊ validated event payload;
- append event to exchange-ledger;
- ensure repo commit exists;
- return commit_sha;
- never mutate historical rows;
- never decide governance;
- never route next actor.

LEDGER_WRITER MUST support append-only semantics.

FORBIDDEN:
- update old event rows
- delete old rows
- rewrite prior statuses
- silently normalize event semantics
- invent missing governance fields

====================================================================================================================
22. DISPATCH REGISTRY CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

Dispatch Registry stores mutable routing state.

Minimum fields:

| FIELD | REQUIRED |
|-------|----------|
| dispatch_id | YES |
| event_id | YES |
| task_id | YES |
| target_actor_role | YES |
| dispatch_status | YES |
| dispatch_attempts | YES |
| last_attempt_time | YES |
| last_error | YES |
| router_version | YES |

Allowed dispatch_status:

- PENDING
- SENT
- ACKNOWLEDGED
- FAILED
- BLOCKED
- EXPIRED

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Dispatch registry tracks delivery.
Exchange-ledger tracks immutable governance and event history.

====================================================================================================================
23. PAYLOAD EXTRACTION RULE
====================================================================================================================

Before routing to CLOUD_CODE,
LEDGER_ROUTER MUST build extracted payload.

Minimum extracted payload:

| FIELD | REQUIRED |
|-------|----------|
| task_id | YES |
| triggering_event_id | YES |
| expected_event | YES |
| approved_scope | YES |
| step_name | YES |
| description | YES |
| relevant_artifact_refs | YES if available |
| relevant_proof_refs | YES if available |
| commit_sha | YES |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
CLOUD_CODE receives extracted payload, not raw full ledger as primary execution contract.

If payload is materialized separately,
it MUST be written into canonical payload container only,
not substituted for exchange-ledger itself.

====================================================================================================================
24. SCHEMA VERSION RULE
====================================================================================================================

schema_version is REQUIRED.

Writer and router MUST validate compatibility.

If incompatible:
- no dispatch
- no autonomous write continuation
- escalate to AUDITOR or OPERATOR

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Schema drift without explicit SSOT update is forbidden.

====================================================================================================================
25. CHAT UI WRITE BAN
====================================================================================================================

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Chat UI write is forbidden as canonical autonomous write path.

ALLOWED ONLY IF:
- explicit operator override
or
- emergency bootstrap before server-side writer exists
or
- incident recovery requiring temporary manual intervention

If Chat UI write is used:
- event_type MUST reflect exceptional path
- writer_actor MUST reflect actual writer
- operator basis MUST be explicit if override used

====================================================================================================================
26. GOVERNANCE LOCKS
====================================================================================================================

The following locks are simultaneously mandatory:

| LOCK | MEANING |
|------|---------|
| SSOT LOCK | no action without current master prompt |
| ROADMAP LOCK | route comes only from master prompt |
| STEP LOCK | no next step before current step accepted |
| AUDIT LOCK | no significant move without auditor governance |
| LEDGER LOCK | no autonomous flow outside exchange-ledger contract |
| ROUTER LOCK | router only executes already-approved handoff |
| WRITER LOCK | writer only appends, never governs |

====================================================================================================================
27. HARD BAN LIST
====================================================================================================================

FORBIDDEN:
- LEDGER_ROUTER writing auditor decisions
- LEDGER_WRITER assigning next actor
- CLOUD_CODE selecting next actor
- ANALYST closing task
- ANALYST or CLOUD_CODE accepting result
- full raw CSV as execution contract for CLOUD_CODE
- mutable ledger history
- delivery retries stored by rewriting old ledger rows
- missing next_actor_role
- missing next_expected_event
- missing routing_decision_basis
- missing commit_sha
- missing schema_version
- free-form unknown event_type
- transition outside allowed transition map
- combined opaque component that mixes writer + router + governance decision
- autonomous continuation without auditor-authored handoff
- canonical dependence on chat memory instead of repo event log

====================================================================================================================
28. MINIMUM PHASE CONTRACT
====================================================================================================================

Phase order remains canonical:

| PHASE | OWNER | OUTPUT |
|-------|-------|--------|
| PRE_ACTION | ANALYST в†’ AUDITOR | proposal and governance decision |
| WRITE | LEDGER_WRITER | append-only repo event + commit_sha |
| ROUTE | LEDGER_ROUTER | target dispatch based on auditor decision |
| EXECUTION | CLOUD_CODE | execution milestones and factual result |
| POST_ACTION | AUDITOR | acceptance / rejection / closure |
| DELIVERY_STATE | DISPATCH_REGISTRY | mutable dispatch tracking |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
No phase may absorb another phaseвЂ™s authority.

====================================================================================================================
29. SUCCESS CONDITION
====================================================================================================================

The contour is canonical only if simultaneously true:

- ledger is append-only
- dispatch state is separate
- auditor assigns next actor
- next_actor_role is present
- next_expected_event is present
- routing_decision_basis is present
- commit_sha is present
- schema_version is present
- router validates transition map
- cloud code receives extracted payload
- writer and router are separate components
- chat UI write is non-canonical fallback only

====================================================================================================================
30. FINAL ENFORCEMENT
====================================================================================================================

РџСЂРѕРґРѕР»Р¶РµРЅРёРµ СЂР°Р·СЂРµС€Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ С‚РѕРіРґР°, РєРѕРіРґР° РѕРґРЅРѕРІСЂРµРјРµРЅРЅРѕ РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅС‹ РІСЃРµ СѓСЃР»РѕРІРёСЏ:

- governance decision written by AUDITOR or OPERATOR override
- event appended by canonical writer path
- repo commit exists
- commit_sha bound to event
- transition valid against canonical map
- router dispatches only assigned next actor
- cloud code receives extracted payload only
- dispatch state stored outside immutable ledger
- post-action acceptance remains with AUDITOR
- no role bypass occurred

Р’Рѕ РІСЃРµС… РѕСЃС‚Р°Р»СЊРЅС‹С… СЃР»СѓС‡Р°СЏС…:
- autonomous continuation forbidden
- routing blocked
- execution blocked
- escalation required

- С„РёРєСЃР°С†РёРё СЂРµС€РµРЅРёР№ РґРѕ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІРёСЏ Рё РїРѕСЃР»Рµ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІРёСЏ;
- РёСЃРєР»СЋС‡РµРЅРёСЏ СЂР°Р±РѕС‚С‹ вЂњРїРѕ РїР°РјСЏС‚Рё С‡Р°С‚Р°вЂќ Р±РµР· machine-readable СЃР»РµРґР°.

====================================================================================================================

Р”Рѕ Р»СЋР±РѕРіРѕ Р·РЅР°С‡РёРјРѕРіРѕ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІРёСЏ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІСѓРµС‚ РѕР±СЏР·Р°С‚РµР»СЊРЅС‹Р№ pre-action loop.

РљР°РЅРѕРЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРёР№ С†РёРєР»:

Р•СЃР»Рё create_commit blocked,
Р° blob/tree СѓР¶Рµ РіРѕС‚РѕРІС‹,
РґРѕРїСѓСЃРєР°РµС‚СЃСЏ РєР°РЅРѕРЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРёР№ fallback:

6. WRITE PATH FALLBACK HIERARCHY
====================================================================================================================

РљР°РЅРѕРЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРёР№ РїРѕСЂСЏРґРѕРє fallback РґР»СЏ commit-stage blocker:

| PRIORITY | FALLBACK PATH | ALLOWED |
|---------|---------------|---------|
| 1 | same content + neutral commit message | YES |
| 2 | same content + alternate low-level write path | YES |
| 3 | same content + contents API style write path | YES |
| 4 | same content + alternate canonical writer contour | YES |
| 5 | operator emergency manual write | ONLY IF EXPLICITLY REQUIRED |

ABSOLUTE RULE:
РџРµСЂРµС…РѕРґ Рє СЂСѓС‡РЅРѕР№ РѕРїРµСЂР°С‚РѕСЂСЃРєРѕР№ Р·Р°РїРёСЃРё Р·Р°РїСЂРµС‰С‘РЅ,

9. RESULT MODEL
====================================================================================================================

РџРѕСЃР»Рµ commit-stage blocker РґРѕРїСѓСЃС‚РёРјС‹ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ С‚СЂРё С‡РµСЃС‚РЅС‹С… СЂРµР·СѓР»СЊС‚Р°С‚Р°.

| RESULT TYPE | MEANING |
|------------|---------|
| clean result | fallback path succeeded and repo-visible proof confirmed |
| conditional result | write succeeded but proof still incomplete |

ABSOLUTE RULE:

10. FAILED STATE DISCIPLINE
====================================================================================================================

Р•СЃР»Рё even fallback path failed,

Action
- С‚РѕС‚ Р¶Рµ С€Р°Рі, С‚Р° Р¶Рµ Р·Р°РїРёСЃСЊ, fallback attempt executed

Proof
- exact failure point
- whether blob/tree/commit/ref succeeded or failed
- repo-visible state unchanged

Result
- failed

Blocker if failed
- exact blocker
- blocker class = WRITE_PATH_BLOCKER
- blocker type = COMMIT_STAGE_BLOCKER or REF_UPDATE_BLOCKER
- next direct corrective action

ABSOLUTE RULE:
РџРѕСЃР»Рµ РІС‚РѕСЂРѕРіРѕ С‡РµСЃС‚РЅРѕ РїРѕРґС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґС‘РЅРЅРѕРіРѕ failed write attempt

Р’ РЅРѕСЂРјР°Р»СЊРЅРѕРј СЂР°Р±РѕС‡РµРј РєРѕРЅС‚СѓСЂРµ РїРѕСЃР»РµРґРЅРµРµ СЃР»РѕРІРѕ Р·Р° РђСѓРґРёС‚РѕСЂРѕРј.

РќРѕ:

СЂР°Р±РѕС‚Р°СЋС‰РёР№ РѕС‚ service account.

3. ABSOLUTE SYSTEM RULES
====================================================================================================================

RULE 1 вЂ” TASK FILE FIRST
Р‘РµР· governance/tasks/<task_id>.json Р·Р°РґР°С‡Р° РЅРµ СЃС‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ materialized.

РёСЃС‚РёРЅРѕР№ СЃС‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ main state.

RULE 7 вЂ” DIRECT CHAT WRITE IS NON-CANONICAL

РћРїРµСЂР°С‚РѕСЂ РјРѕР¶РµС‚ Р·Р°РїСѓСЃРєР°С‚СЊ workflow,

9. POST-EXECUTION ROUTING RULES
====================================================================================================================

РџРѕСЃР»Рµ ACTION_COMPLETED
РєР°РЅРѕРЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРёР№ РјР°СЂС€СЂСѓС‚:

в†’ ANALYST / VERIFIER
в†’ AUDITOR
в†’ closure materialization contour

РџРѕСЃР»Рµ TASK_PROPOSED:

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Р•СЃР»Рё РґРµР№СЃС‚РІСѓСЋС‰РёР№ РєР°РЅРѕРЅ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РµР№ РІРµСЂСЃРёРё Р·Р°РєСЂРµРїР»СЏРµС‚ TASK_CLOSED Р·Р° AUDITOR,

- СЃР°Рј AUDITOR, РµСЃР»Рё СЌС‚Рѕ Р·Р°РєСЂРµРїР»РµРЅРѕ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІСѓСЋС‰РёРј workflow contract;
РёР»Рё
- LEDGER_WRITER, РЅРѕ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РєР°Рє С‚РµС…РЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРѕРµ server-side materialization СѓР¶Рµ РїСЂРёРЅСЏС‚РѕРіРѕ auditor closure decision.

13.3
РџРѕРІС‚РѕСЂРЅС‹Р№ TASK_CLOSED РґРѕР»Р¶РµРЅ Р±Р»РѕРєРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊСЃСЏ РёРґРµРјРїРѕС‚РµРЅС‚РЅРѕР№ Р·Р°С‰РёС‚РѕР№.

13.4
ANALYST / EXECUTOR / CLOUD_CODE РЅРµ РёРјРµСЋС‚ РїСЂР°РІР° РїРёСЃР°С‚СЊ TASK_CLOSED.

====================================================================================================================

====================================================================================================================

analyst-task-writer.yml С„РёРєСЃРёСЂСѓРµС‚СЃСЏ РєР°Рє mandatory missing server-side contour,
РєРѕС‚РѕСЂС‹Р№ Р·Р°РєСЂС‹РІР°РµС‚ РЅРµ СѓРґРѕР±СЃС‚РІРѕ,

- РїРµСЂРµРґР°РІР°С‚СЊ Р·Р°РґР°С‡Сѓ РґР°Р»СЊС€Рµ РІ audit / ledger contour.

Р”Рѕ РµРіРѕ РїРѕСЏРІР»РµРЅРёСЏ:

- РЅРѕРІРѕРіРѕ РїРµСЂРµС…РѕРґР°

РѕР±СЏР·Р°С‚РµР»СЊРЅР° РѕС‚РґРµР»СЊРЅР°СЏ РєРѕР»РѕРЅРєР°:

РќР°Р·РЅР°С‡РµРЅРёРµ СЌС‚РѕР№ РєРѕР»РѕРЅРєРё:

- РґР°С‚СЊ С‡РµР»РѕРІРµРєСѓ РїРѕРЅСЏС‚РЅСѓСЋ СЂР°СЃС€РёС„СЂРѕРІРєСѓ С‚РѕРіРѕ, С‡С‚Рѕ СЂРµР°Р»СЊРЅРѕ РѕР·РЅР°С‡Р°РµС‚ СЃРѕСЃС‚РѕСЏРЅРёРµ СЃРёСЃС‚РµРјС‹.

ABSOLUTE RULE:

РµСЃР»Рё РґР»СЏ РЅРµРіРѕ РЅРµ СѓРєР°Р·Р°РЅ СЂСѓСЃСЃРєРёР№ РїРµСЂРµРІРѕРґ / СЂСѓСЃСЃРєРёР№ РѕРїРµСЂР°С†РёРѕРЅРЅС‹Р№ СЃРјС‹СЃР».

18. STATUS EXTENSION GOVERNANCE RULE
====================================================================================================================

Р•СЃР»Рё РІ СЃРёСЃС‚РµРјРµ РІРѕР·РЅРёРєР°РµС‚ СЃРёС‚СѓР°С†РёСЏ, РєРѕС‚РѕСЂР°СЏ:

- РЅРµ РїРѕРєСЂС‹РІР°РµС‚СЃСЏ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РёРјРё event_type;
- РЅРµ РїРѕРєСЂС‹РІР°РµС‚СЃСЏ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РёРјРё status values;
- РїРѕРєСЂС‹РІР°РµС‚СЃСЏ СЃР»РёС€РєРѕРј РіСЂСѓР±Рѕ;
- РїСЂРёРІРѕРґРёС‚ Рє Р»РѕР¶РЅРѕР№ РёРЅС‚РµСЂРїСЂРµС‚Р°С†РёРё;
- С‚СЂРµР±СѓРµС‚ РѕС‚РґРµР»СЊРЅРѕРіРѕ СЃРѕСЃС‚РѕСЏРЅРёСЏ verification / retry / blocked / rollback / degraded path;

С‚Рѕ РїСЂРёРјРµРЅСЏРµС‚СЃСЏ СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰Р°СЏ РїСЂРѕС†РµРґСѓСЂР°.

STEP 1
AUDITOR С„РёРєСЃРёСЂСѓРµС‚, С‡С‚Рѕ РѕР±РЅР°СЂСѓР¶РµРЅ status gap.

STEP 2
РћРїСЂРµРґРµР»СЏРµС‚СЃСЏ, РЅСѓР¶РµРЅ Р»Рё:
- РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ event_type,
- РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ status,
- РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ transition,
- Р»РёР±Рѕ РґРѕСЃС‚Р°С‚РѕС‡РЅРѕ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РµРіРѕ РЅР°Р±РѕСЂР°.

STEP 3
Р•СЃР»Рё РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РґРµР№СЃС‚РІРёС‚РµР»СЊРЅРѕ РЅСѓР¶РµРЅ,
AUDITOR РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ РѕРїСЂРµРґРµР»РёС‚СЊ:

- canonical name;
- russian_translation;
- meaning;
- allowed_roles / who_may_set;
- lifecycle phase;
- proof requirements;
- terminal or non-terminal behavior;
- transition rules.

STEP 4
РќРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РґРѕР±Р°РІР»СЏРµС‚СЃСЏ РІ EXTENSION REGISTRY.

STEP 5
Р”Рѕ materialization РІ СЃРёСЃС‚РµРјРµ
РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РќР• СЃС‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ operationally active.

STEP 6
Materialization РѕР·РЅР°С‡Р°РµС‚ РѕР±СЏР·Р°С‚РµР»СЊРЅРѕРµ РґРѕР±Р°РІР»РµРЅРёРµ РІ:
- SSOT / master prompt / add-on;
- workflow prompts;
- validators;
- allowlists;
- lifecycle_manager transitions;
- ledger-router routing rules;
- analyst / auditor / executor runner logic РїСЂРё РЅРµРѕР±С…РѕРґРёРјРѕСЃС‚Рё.

====================================================================================================================
19. WHO MAY INTRODUCE NEW STATUSES
====================================================================================================================

19.1 AUDITOR
РўРѕР»СЊРєРѕ AUDITOR РёРјРµРµС‚ РїСЂР°РІРѕ РєР°РЅРѕРЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРё РІРІРѕРґРёС‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ status / event_type / transition.

AUDITOR РјРѕР¶РµС‚:
- СѓС‚РІРµСЂРґРёС‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ;
- РѕС‚РєР»РѕРЅРёС‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ;
- РїСЂРёР·РЅР°С‚СЊ, С‡С‚Рѕ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РµРіРѕ РЅР°Р±РѕСЂР° РґРѕСЃС‚Р°С‚РѕС‡РЅРѕ;
- РїРµСЂРµРІРµСЃС‚Рё РїСЂРµРґР»РѕР¶РµРЅРЅС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РІ pending / draft / rejected state.

19.2 ANALYST
ANALYST РјРѕР¶РµС‚:
- РѕР±РЅР°СЂСѓР¶РёС‚СЊ gap;
- РїСЂРµРґР»РѕР¶РёС‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ;
- РѕРїРёСЃР°С‚СЊ, РїРѕС‡РµРјСѓ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РёР№ РЅР°Р±РѕСЂ РЅРµРґРѕСЃС‚Р°С‚РѕС‡РµРЅ;
- РїРѕРґРіРѕС‚РѕРІРёС‚СЊ draft definition.

ANALYST РќР• РјРѕР¶РµС‚:
- РєР°РЅРѕРЅРёР·РёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ СЃР°РјРѕСЃС‚РѕСЏС‚РµР»СЊРЅРѕ;
- РёСЃРїРѕР»СЊР·РѕРІР°С‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ РєР°Рє operationally valid,
  РїРѕРєР° РµРіРѕ РЅРµ СѓС‚РІРµСЂРґРёР» AUDITOR.

19.3 EXECUTOR / CLOUD_CODE
EXECUTOR / CLOUD_CODE РЅРµ РёРјРµРµС‚ РїСЂР°РІР° СЃР°РјРѕРІРѕР»СЊРЅРѕ РїСЂРёРґСѓРјС‹РІР°С‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Рµ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃС‹.

Р•СЃР»Рё executor СЃС‚Р°Р»РєРёРІР°РµС‚СЃСЏ СЃ РЅРµРїРѕРґРґРµСЂР¶РёРІР°РµРјРѕР№ СЃРёС‚СѓР°С†РёРµР№,
РѕРЅ РѕР±СЏР·Р°РЅ РёСЃРїРѕР»СЊР·РѕРІР°С‚СЊ СѓР¶Рµ СЂР°Р·СЂРµС€С‘РЅРЅС‹Р№ fallback path:
- VALIDATION_FAILED
- EMERGENCY_BLOCKED
- RESULT_REJECTED
- РёРЅРѕР№ СѓР¶Рµ РєР°РЅРѕРЅРёР·РёСЂРѕРІР°РЅРЅС‹Р№ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ,
РІ Р·Р°РІРёСЃРёРјРѕСЃС‚Рё РѕС‚ С‚РµРєСѓС‰РµРіРѕ РєРѕРЅС‚СЂР°РєС‚Р°.

====================================================================================================================
20. STATUS MATERIALIZATION RULE
====================================================================================================================

РќРѕРІС‹Р№ status / event_type / transition СЃС‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ Р°РєС‚РёРІРЅС‹Рј С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РµСЃР»Рё РѕРґРЅРѕРІСЂРµРјРµРЅРЅРѕ РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅС‹ РІСЃРµ СѓСЃР»РѕРІРёСЏ:

1. РћРЅ РІРЅРµСЃС‘РЅ РІ СЂРµРµСЃС‚СЂ.
2. Р”Р»СЏ РЅРµРіРѕ СѓРєР°Р·Р°РЅ russian_translation.
3. РћРЅ СѓС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґС‘РЅ AUDITOR.
4. РћРЅ РґРѕР±Р°РІР»РµРЅ РІ SSOT / add-on.
5. РћРЅ РґРѕР±Р°РІР»РµРЅ РІ validators / allowlists.
6. РћРЅ РґРѕР±Р°РІР»РµРЅ РІ routing / lifecycle logic, РµСЃР»Рё С‚СЂРµР±СѓРµС‚СЃСЏ.

Р•СЃР»Рё С…РѕС‚СЏ Р±С‹ РѕРґРЅРѕ СѓСЃР»РѕРІРёРµ РЅРµ РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРѕ:

- РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°РµС‚ РёР»Рё РЅРµ РїСЂРёРЅРёРјР°РµС‚ СЂРµР·СѓР»СЊС‚Р°С‚;

====================================================================================================================
8. POST-ACTION CANON
====================================================================================================================

РџРѕСЃР»Рµ execution РґРµР№СЃС‚РІСѓРµС‚ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ С‚Р°РєРѕР№ canonical flow:

EXECUTOR statement
в†’ ANALYST / VERIFIER verification outcome
в†’ AUDITOR acceptance / rejection decision
в†’ closure routing

If accepted:
- accepted result exists
- task may proceed to closure contour
- next planning starts only after closure state is materialized if required by canon

If not accepted:
- current task remains open
- new task is not opened
- ANALYST prepares corrective proposal for the same task unless canon explicitly says otherwise

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Not accepted result does not open a new task by default.

====================================================================================================================
9. TASK_CLOSED вЂ” CONSOLIDATED RULE
====================================================================================================================

Р•РґРёРЅСЃС‚РІРµРЅРЅР°СЏ active interpretation С‚Р°РєР°СЏ:

TASK_CLOSED is NOT an auditor-owned decision event.
TASK_CLOSED is a terminal closure materialization event.

Meaning:
- AUDITOR decides whether result is accepted or rejected;
- after valid acceptance, routing may send the task into closure contour;
- closure contour / LEDGER_WRITER materializes TASK_CLOSED;
- this terminal event is technical/systemic closure materialization,
  not the semantic acceptance decision itself.

ABSOLUTE RULE:
If older text says "AUDITOR writes TASK_CLOSED" directly,
that text is superseded by this consolidated rule.

====================================================================================================================
10. ANALYST SPLIT вЂ” CONSOLIDATED RULE
====================================================================================================================

ANALYST split is active and mandatory:

ANALYST / PLANNER:
- planning
- proposal
- materialization
- correction planning

ANALYST / VERIFIER:
- factual verification
- main-state proof check
- verification outcome

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Verification is not optional commentary.
Verification is a formal lifecycle gate.

====================================================================================================================
11. ROUTING AFTER ACCEPTANCE
====================================================================================================================

РџРѕСЃР»Рµ RESULT_ACCEPTED РјР°СЂС€СЂСѓС‚ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ С‚Р°РєРѕР№:

AUDITOR accepted result
в†’ next_actor_role = closure contour / LEDGER_WRITER
в†’ TASK_CLOSED materialized
в†’ next planning cycle may begin

РџРѕСЃР»Рµ RESULT_REJECTED РјР°СЂС€СЂСѓС‚ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ С‚Р°РєРѕР№:

AUDITOR rejected result
в†’ next_actor_role = ANALYST
в†’ corrective proposal for same task
в†’ same task continues

====================================================================================================================
12. MINIMUM ACTIVE FORMULAS
====================================================================================================================

PLANNING:
ANALYST / PLANNER chooses next valid step from MASTER PROMPT

VERIFICATION:
ANALYST / VERIFIER confirms repo-visible proof

ACCEPTANCE:
AUDITOR accepts or rejects verified result

CLOSURE:
CLOSURE CONTOUR materializes TASK_CLOSED

OVERRIDE:
OPERATOR may override normal contour only explicitly

====================================================================================================================
13. SUPERSEDED INTERPRETATIONS
====================================================================================================================

The following older interpretations are superseded in the scope of conflict:

- AUDITOR as owner of TASK_CLOSED
- any chain without ANALYST / VERIFIER gate
- any acceptance rule that allows executor claim as sufficient proof
- any closure rule that merges acceptance decision and closure materialization into one responsibility
- any reading where ANALYST is not split into PLANNER and VERIFIER after the new add-on set

====================================================================================================================

Р•СЃР»Рё РІ РґРѕРєСѓРјРµРЅС‚Рµ РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅС‹ РѕРґРЅРѕРІСЂРµРјРµРЅРЅРѕ:
- СЃС‚Р°СЂР°СЏ role formula
- Рё РґР°РЅРЅР°СЏ consolidated role formula

С‚Рѕ active interpretation РІСЃРµРіРґР° Р±РµСЂС‘С‚СЃСЏ РёР· РґР°РЅРЅРѕРіРѕ consolidated add-on.

This add-on exists specifically to prevent ambiguity.

15. FINAL ENFORCEMENT
====================================================================================================================

РЎ СЌС‚РѕРіРѕ РјРѕРјРµРЅС‚Р° РµРґРёРЅСЃС‚РІРµРЅРЅР°СЏ РґРѕРїСѓСЃС‚РёРјР°СЏ active С‚СЂР°РєС‚РѕРІРєР° С‚Р°РєРѕРІР°:

- task file must be materialized before execution;
- EXECUTOR performs only approved work;
- ANALYST / VERIFIER confirms repo-visible proof;
- AUDITOR accepts or rejects only after verification;
- CLOSURE CONTOUR / LEDGER_WRITER materializes TASK_CLOSED;
- OPERATOR is override authority, not normal delivery proxy.

2. SUPERSEDED LEGACY FORMULATIONS
====================================================================================================================

Р’СЃРµ Р±РѕР»РµРµ СЂР°РЅРЅРёРµ С„РѕСЂРјСѓР»РёСЂРѕРІРєРё РІРЅСѓС‚СЂРё MASTER PROMPT, РєРѕС‚РѕСЂС‹Рµ СѓС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґР°СЋС‚ С…РѕС‚СЏ Р±С‹ РѕРґРЅРѕ РёР· СЃР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РµРіРѕ,

====================================================================================================================
3. TASK_CLOSED CLEAN RULE
====================================================================================================================

TASK_CLOSED now has only one valid interpretation:

- semantic acceptance decision = AUDITOR responsibility
- terminal closure materialization = CLOSURE CONTOUR / LEDGER_WRITER responsibility

Therefore:
- AUDITOR may accept the result
- AUDITOR may authorize progression to closure
- but TASK_CLOSED as terminal system event belongs to closure contour

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Any reading that merges acceptance and TASK_CLOSED ownership into a single auditor-owned action is invalid.

====================================================================================================================
4. VERIFICATION CLEAN RULE
====================================================================================================================

Verification is a mandatory lifecycle gate, not commentary.

Only ANALYST / VERIFIER may issue verification outcome.
AUDITOR may only use that verification outcome, not replace it.

Minimum active verification chain:

ACTION_COMPLETED
в†’ repo-visible main read
в†’ proof_target comparison
в†’ verification outcome
в†’ acceptance / rejection decision

ABSOLUTE RULE:
No verification = no RESULT_ACCEPTED.

====================================================================================================================
5. TASK MATERIALIZATION CLEAN RULE
====================================================================================================================

Task file materialization remains mandatory.

Operational readiness requires all of the following:
- roadmap-valid step chosen by ANALYST / PLANNER
- task file exists in governance/tasks/<task_id>.json
- pre-action approval exists

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Proposal text alone is not operational readiness.

- FULL ROLE / VERIFICATION / CLOSURE TEXTUAL CONSOLIDATION

====================================================================================================================
14. CANONICAL SA DEVELOPMENT FLOW
====================================================================================================================

Р•РґРёРЅС‹Р№ РєР°РЅРѕРЅРёС‡РµСЃРєРёР№ flow СЂР°Р·СЂР°Р±РѕС‚РєРё С‚Р°РєРѕРІ:

====================================================================================================================
15. NON-CANONICAL PATH CLASSIFICATION
====================================================================================================================

РЎР»РµРґСѓСЋС‰РёРµ РїСѓС‚Рё СЃС‡РёС‚Р°СЋС‚СЃСЏ non-canonical:

- direct chat-to-GitHub write as normal model;
- manual secret-based repo write from chat as steady-state path;
- operator-as-normal-proxy model;
- completion claim without repo-visible SA-materialized artifact where SA is required.

ABSOLUTE RULE:
Non-canonical path may exist temporarily.
It must not be confused with target operating model.

====================================================================================================================
16. SUCCESS CONDITION
====================================================================================================================

SA model СЃС‡РёС‚Р°РµС‚СЃСЏ СЃРѕР±Р»СЋРґС‘РЅРЅРѕР№ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РµСЃР»Рё РѕРґРЅРѕРІСЂРµРјРµРЅРЅРѕ РёСЃС‚РёРЅРЅРѕ:

- significant writes go through server-side contour;
- task file materialization is SA-first;
- ledger / closure writes are SA-first or explicitly bootstrapped exception;
- direct chat write is treated as exception, not norm;
- secrets stay in server-side privileged contour;
- verification remains separate from SA write success;
- acceptance remains separate from execution success.

====================================================================================================================
17. SHORT CANONICAL FORM
====================================================================================================================

SA-FIRST FORMULA:

reason in chat
в†’ write on server side
в†’ verify in repo
в†’ accept by audit
в†’ close through closure contour

CHAT FORMULA:
chat plans
chat audits
chat explains
chat generates copy-ready payload

SA FORMULA:
SA writes
SA executes
SA materializes
SA uses privileged environment

====================================================================================================================
18. FINAL ENFORCEMENT
====================================================================================================================

РЎ СЌС‚РѕРіРѕ РјРѕРјРµРЅС‚Р° РµРґРёРЅСЃС‚РІРµРЅРЅР°СЏ РґРѕРїСѓСЃС‚РёРјР°СЏ С‚СЂР°РєС‚РѕРІРєР° С‚Р°РєРѕРІР°:

- normal development / write / materialization path = SA-first;
- direct chat write = exception only;
- task file materialization must become server-side contour responsibility;
- significant repo writes must not rely on chat as normal engine;
- verification and acceptance remain separate from SA write success.
